## Idea

An **isomorphism** in a [precategory](category-theory.precategories.md) `C` is a
morphism `f : x → y` in `C` for which there exists a morphism `g : y → x` such
that `f ∘ g ＝ id` and `g ∘ f ＝ id`.

## Definitions

### The predicate of being an isomorphism in a precategory

### Isomorphisms in a precategory

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2210" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="2217" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2217" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="2221" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2222" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="2226" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2226" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="2230" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2232" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="2237" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="2241" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2242" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2242" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="2245" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2247" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="2260" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2222" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="2264" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2226" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="2267" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="2271" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2272" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2272" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="2275" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2275" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="2278" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2280" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="2297" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2242" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="2299" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="2303" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Examples

### The identity isomorphisms

For any object `x : A`, the identity morphism `id_x : hom x x` is an isomorphism
from `x` to `x` since `id_x ∘ id_x = id_x` (it is its own inverse).

<pre class="Agda"><a id="3696" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="3703" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3703" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="3707" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3708" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3708" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="3712" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3712" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="3716" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3718" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="3723" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="3727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3728" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3728" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="3731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3733" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="3746" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3708" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="3750" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3712" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="3753" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="3757" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3758" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3758" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="3761" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3763" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="3780" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3728" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="3782" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="3786" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="3795" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3795" class="Function">is-iso-id-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="3822" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="3828" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1053" class="Function">is-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="3848" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3728" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="3851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3852" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7302" class="Function">id-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="3872" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3728" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="3875" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3876" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3758" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="3878" class="Symbol">})</a>

  <a id="4267" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="4272" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4165" class="Function">id-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="4292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4294" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3795" class="Function">is-iso-id-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a>
</pre>
### Equalities induce isomorphisms

An equality between objects `x y : A` gives rise to an isomorphism between them.
This is because, by the J-rule, it is enough to construct an isomorphism given
`refl : x ＝ x`, from `x` to itself. We take the identity morphism as such an
isomorphism.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4621" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4628" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4628" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="4632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4633" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4633" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="4637" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4637" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="4641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4643" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4648" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Properties

### Being an isomorphism is a proposition

Let `f : hom x y` and suppose `g g' : hom y x` are both two-sided inverses to
`f`. It is enough to show that `g = g'` since the equalities are
[propositions](foundation-core.propositions.md) (since the hom-types are sets).
But we have the following chain of equalities:
`g = g ∘ id_y = g ∘ (f ∘ g') = (g ∘ f) ∘ g' = id_x ∘ g' = g'`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5575" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5582" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5582" class="Module">_</a>

### Equality of isomorphism is equality of their underlying morphisms

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7084" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7091" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7091" class="Module">_</a>

### The type of isomorphisms form a set

The type of isomorphisms between objects `x y : A` is a
[subtype](foundation-core.subtypes.md) of the [set](foundation-core.sets.md)
`hom x y` since being an isomorphism is a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7660" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7667" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7667" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="7671" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7672" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7672" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="7676" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7676" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="7680" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7682" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="7687" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="7691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7692" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7692" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="7695" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7697" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="7710" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7672" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="7714" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7676" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="7717" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7721" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7722" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7722" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="7725" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7725" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="7728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7730" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="7747" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7692" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="7749" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Isomorphisms are closed under composition

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8161" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8168" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8168" class="Module">_</a>

  <a id="11683" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="11688" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11631" class="Function">comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="11710" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11712" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11202" class="Function">hom-comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a>

  <a id="13520" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13520" class="Function">is-iso-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13548" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="13554" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13555" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13555" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="13558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13560" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2312" class="Function">iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13577" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13195" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="13580" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13225" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="13583" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13228" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="13585" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13587" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="13593" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1053" class="Function">is-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13613" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13195" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="13616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13617" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2752" class="Function">hom-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13642" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13195" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="13645" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13555" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="13647" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13651" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13520" class="Function">is-iso-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13679" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13679" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="13682" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="13688" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2639" class="Function">is-iso-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13712" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13195" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="13715" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13716" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13265" class="Function">inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="13737" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13679" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="13739" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Groupoid laws of isomorphisms in precategories

#### Composition of isomorphisms is associative

<pre class="Agda"><a id="14739" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14746" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14746" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="15169" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7186" class="Function">eq-iso-eq-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="15196" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14771" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a>
      <a id="15205" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15207" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11631" class="Function">comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="15229" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14771" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="15232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15233" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11631" class="Function">comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="15255" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14771" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="15258" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14839" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="15261" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14874" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="15263" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15265" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14909" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="15267" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="15275" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15277" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11631" class="Function">comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="15299" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14771" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="15302" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14839" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="15305" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15306" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11631" class="Function">comp-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="15328" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14771" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="15331" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14874" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="15334" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#14909" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="15336" class="Symbol">))</a>

### The inverse operation is a fibered involution on isomorphisms

<pre class="Agda"><a id="16522" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16529" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16529" class="Module">_</a>

    <a id="16966" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5107" class="Function">is-equiv-is-invertibleᵉ</a>
      <a id="16996" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="16998" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13265" class="Function">inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17019" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16554" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="17021" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="17029" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17031" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16592" class="Function">is-fibered-involution-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a><a id="17073" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="17081" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="17083" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16592" class="Function">is-fibered-involution-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a><a id="17125" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="17130" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17130" class="Function">equiv-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17157" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="17163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17164" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17164" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17167" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17167" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="17170" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17172" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17189" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16554" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="17191" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17193" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17195" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2312" class="Function">iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17212" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16554" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="17215" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17164" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="17218" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17167" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="17221" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2662" class="Function Operator">≃ᵉ</a> <a id="17224" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2312" class="Function">iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17241" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16554" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="17244" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17167" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="17247" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17164" class="Bound">xᵉ</a>
  <a id="17252" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#697" class="Field">pr1ᵉ</a> <a id="17257" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17130" class="Function">equiv-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17284" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17286" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#13265" class="Function">inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17307" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16554" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a>
  <a id="17312" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#711" class="Field">pr2ᵉ</a> <a id="17317" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17130" class="Function">equiv-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="17344" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17346" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#16814" class="Function">is-equiv-inv-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a>
</pre>
### A morphism `f` is an isomorphism if and only if precomposition by `f` is an equivalence

**Proof:** If `f` is an isomorphism with inverse `f⁻¹`, then precomposing with
`f⁻¹` is an inverse of precomposing with `f`. The only interesting direction is
therefore the converse.

Suppose that precomposing with `f` is an equivalence, for any object `z`. Then

```text
  - ∘ f : hom y x → hom x x
```

is an equivalence. In particular, there is a unique morphism `g : y → x` such
that `g ∘ f ＝ id`. Thus we have a retraction of `f`. To see that `g` is also a
section, note that the map

```text
  - ∘ f : hom y y → hom x y
```

is an equivalence. In particular, it is injective. Therefore it suffices to show
that `(f ∘ g) ∘ f ＝ id ∘ f`. To see this, we calculate

```text
  (f ∘ g) ∘ f ＝ f ∘ (g ∘ f) ＝ f ∘ id ＝ f ＝ id ∘ f.
```

This completes the proof.

  <a id="22192" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22193" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22193" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="22197" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22197" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="22201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22203" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="22208" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="22212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22213" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22218" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22231" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22193" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="22235" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22197" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="22238" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22242" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22243" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22243" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="22246" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22246" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="22249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22251" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22268" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="22270" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="22274" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22275" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22275" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="22278" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22280" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2312" class="Function">iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22297" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22300" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22243" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="22303" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22246" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="22305" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22310" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="22313" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22315" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22332" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="22334" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22338" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22347" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22347" class="Function">is-equiv-precomp-hom-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22385" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="22391" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1553" class="Function">is-equivᵉ</a> <a id="22401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22402" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9887" class="Function">precomp-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22427" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22431" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2554" class="Function">hom-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22452" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22455" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22275" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="22457" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22459" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a><a id="22461" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="22465" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22347" class="Function">is-equiv-precomp-hom-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22503" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="22509" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21563" class="Function">is-equiv-precomp-hom-is-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22550" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22553" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22554" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2639" class="Function">is-iso-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22578" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22581" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22275" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="22583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22585" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a>

  <a id="22591" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22591" class="Function">equiv-precomp-hom-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22626" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="22632" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4999" class="Function">hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22649" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22652" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22246" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="22655" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a> <a id="22658" href="foundation-core.equivalences%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2662" class="Function Operator">≃ᵉ</a> <a id="22661" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4999" class="Function">hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22678" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22681" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22243" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="22684" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a>
  <a id="22689" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22591" class="Function">equiv-precomp-hom-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22724" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="22730" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21904" class="Function">equiv-precomp-hom-is-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22768" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22772" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2639" class="Function">is-iso-iso-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="22796" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22213" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="22799" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22275" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="22801" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22803" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22310" class="Bound">zᵉ</a>
</pre>
### A morphism `f` is an isomorphism if and only if postcomposition by `f` is an equivalence

**Proof:** If `f` is an isomorphism with inverse `f⁻¹`, then postcomposing with
`f⁻¹` is an inverse of postcomposing with `f`. The only interesting direction is
therefore the converse.

Suppose that postcomposing with `f` is an equivalence, for any object `z`. Then

```text
  f ∘ - : hom y x → hom y y
```

is an equivalence. In particular, there is a unique morphism `g : y → x` such
that `f ∘ g ＝ id`. Thus we have a section of `f`. To see that `g` is also a
retraction, note that the map

```text
  f ∘ - : hom x x → hom x y
```

is an equivalence. In particular, it is injective. Therefore it suffices to show
that `f ∘ (g ∘ f) ＝ f ∘ id`. To see this, we calculate

```text
  f ∘ (g ∘ f) ＝ (f ∘ g) ∘ f ＝ id ∘ f ＝ f ＝ f ∘ id.
```

This completes the proof.

### When `hom x y` is a proposition, The type of isomorphisms from `x` to `y` is a proposition

The type of isomorphisms between objects `x y : A` is a subtype of `hom x y`, so
when this type is a proposition, then the type of isomorphisms from `x` to `y`
form a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28636" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="28643" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28643" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="28647" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28648" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28648" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="28652" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28652" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="28656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28658" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="28663" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28666" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28666" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="28669" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28671" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="28684" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28648" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="28688" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28652" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="28691" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="28695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28696" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28696" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="28699" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28699" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="28702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28704" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4836" class="Function">obj-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="28721" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28666" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a><a id="28723" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="28727" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28736" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28736" class="Function">is-prop-iso-is-prop-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="28773" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="28995" href="foundation-core.propositions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1041" class="Function">is-propᵉ</a> <a id="29004" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29005" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4999" class="Function">hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="29022" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28666" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="29025" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28696" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="29028" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28699" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="29030" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29032" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29034" href="foundation-core.propositions%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1181" class="Function">Propᵉ</a> <a id="29040" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28652" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a>

    <a id="29206" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#28736" class="Function">is-prop-iso-is-prop-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="29243" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29180" class="Bound">is-prop-hom-C-x-yᵉ</a>

### When `hom x y` and `hom y x` are propositions, it suffices to provide a morphism in each direction to construct an isomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="29407" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="29414" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29414" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="29418" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29419" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29419" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="29423" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29423" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="29427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29429" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="29434" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="29436" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29437" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29437" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="29440" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29442" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="29455" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29419" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="29459" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29423" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="29462" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="30947" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4999" class="Function">hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="30964" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29437" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="30967" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29470" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="30970" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29467" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="30973" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="31057" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#30015" class="Function">iso-is-prop-hom-Precategory&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="31087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31088" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31036" class="Bound">is-prop-hom-Cᵉ</a> <a id="31103" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29467" class="Bound">xᵉ</a> <a id="31106" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29467" class="Bound">xᵉ</a><a id="31108" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31110" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31111" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#31036" class="Bound">is-prop-hom-Cᵉ</a> <a id="31126" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29470" class="Bound">yᵉ</a> <a id="31129" href="category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#29470" class="Bound">yᵉ</a><a id="31131" class="Symbol">)</a>
